-----title
金华（东阳）
-----detail

-----end

-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0cc60d789656483e82f196c8d60d5fb7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0cc60d789656483e82f196c8d60d5fb7");'><span id='0cc60d789656483e82f196c8d60d5fb7_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=855&endYear=855')">855年</a>　秋，游扬州，献诗崔铉。作品：献淮南崔相公。<div id='poem_826045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_826045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/826045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>献淮南崔相公</a><span class='authorDate'>（855年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_826045")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_826045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_826045'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_826045'>天临黄合如秋净，日照洪钧若昼清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_826045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_826045'>虎帐坐分真宰气，象筵吹出泰阶声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_826045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_826045'>云霞自入淮王梦，风月谁含炀帝情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_826045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_826045'>见说蓬莱百王发，玉皇吟出广陵城<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_826045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_826045'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_826045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_826045'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_826045_0'>⑴ 此见《永乐大典》卷二七四四「八灰」「崔」字「崔某」条引《维扬志》，四函三十四册。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_826045_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8ee3ac2e149f43c2a93f234c4c87ba10_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8ee3ac2e149f43c2a93f234c4c87ba10");'><span id='8ee3ac2e149f43c2a93f234c4c87ba10_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>，32岁</div><div id='8ee3ac2e149f43c2a93f234c4c87ba10' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，至扬州，遇陈黯，归还文卷，激其再举，相欢月馀而别。陈黯请罗隐代为感谢卢浔，并告知东归决心，永不再举；或拜谒镇扬州的令狐绹。作品：广陵秋夜读进士常修三篇因题。<div id='poem_37831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广陵秋夜读进士常修三篇因题</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37831")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37831'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37831'>入蜀归吴三首诗，藏于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_37831", 37831, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>笥箧</span>重于师。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37831'>剑关夜读相如听，瓜步秋吟炀帝悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37831'>景物也知输健笔，时情谁不许高枝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37831'>明年二月春风里，江岛闲人慰所思。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37831_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37831'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，在扬州作赋。作品：迷楼赋。<div id='poem_1377583' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377583' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377583?labeling=true' target='_blank'>迷楼赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377583")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377583_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377583'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377583'>岁在甲申。余不幸于春官兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377583_comment'></div>凭羸车以东驱。□魏阙之三千兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377583_comment'></div>得随家之故都。乔木拱立以不语兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377583_comment'></div>繄今昔之自离。慨馀基之未平兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377583_comment'></div>曰迷楼而在斯。迷楼者何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377583_comment'></div>炀帝所制。炀袭文后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377583_comment'></div>天下无事。谓春物繁好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377583_comment'></div>不足以开吾视。谓春风懒慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377583_comment'></div>不足以欣吾志。斯志既炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377583_comment'></div>斯楼乃峙。榱桷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1377583", 1377583, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>沈檀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377583_comment'></div>栋梁梓。将使乎旁不通乎日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377583_comment'></div>外不见乎天地。然后朝奏于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377583_comment'></div>寝食于此。君王欲左右有粉黛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377583_comment'></div>君王欲左右有郑卫。君王欲问乎百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377583_comment'></div>曰百姓有相。君王欲问乎四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377583_comment'></div>曰四方有将。于是相秉君恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377583_comment'></div>将侮君权。百姓庶位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377583_comment'></div>万户千门。且不知隋炀帝迷于楼乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377583_comment'></div>迷于人乎。若迷于楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377583_comment'></div>则楼本土木。亦无亲属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377583_comment'></div>纵有所迷。何爽君德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377583_comment'></div>吾意隋炀帝非迷于楼。而人迷炀帝于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377583_comment'></div>故曰迷楼。然后见生灵意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377583_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1377583_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b0d06341c8864cf7878973982063995c_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=881&endYear=881')">881年</a>，49岁</div><div id='81dea3e2ae744702a7615cd19f87e161' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: id='poem_sentence_1_37878'>九里楼台牵翡翠，两行鸳鹭踏真珠。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37878'>歌听丽句秦云咽，诗转新题<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_37878'>惆怅晋阳星拆后，世间兵革地荒芜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37878_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37878'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37878_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在扬州送光禄卿崔某，有诗。作品：送光禄崔卿赴阙。<div id='poem_37981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37981' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377607'>长官镂笔才清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377607_comment'></div>探骊价重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377607_comment'></div>因循世态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377607_comment'></div>放荡宦游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377607_comment'></div>剧谭以鸡肋况时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377607_comment'></div>偶对以马曹当职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377607_comment'></div>而自黄尘北望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377607_comment'></div>翠辇南巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377607_comment'></div>张掾投<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作抽）</span>簪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377607_comment'></div>虽离齐邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377607_comment'></div>陶公染翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377607_comment'></div>本恸晋朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377607_comment'></div>于半郊半郭之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377607_comment'></div>有一咏一觞之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377607_comment'></div>为谋甚逸。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377607_comment'></div>晴阳媚景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377607_comment'></div>别受指撝。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377607_comment'></div>牙弦久绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377607_comment'></div>秦缶增惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377595_comment'></div>斯人以当年不偶于良知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377595_comment'></div>晚岁遂成其永恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377595_comment'></div>况某早将此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377595_comment'></div>以戒前车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377595_comment'></div>至愿蹉跎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377595_comment'></div>年光老大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377595_comment'></div>向秦庭而屡泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377595_comment'></div>抱楚足以频伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377595_comment'></div>中间辄以所著谗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377595_comment'></div>上干阍吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377595_comment'></div>近见某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377595_comment'></div>伏知阁下爰哀弱植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377595_comment'></div>俯降深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377595_comment'></div>回日月于壶中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377595_comment'></div>展方书于肘后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377595_comment'></div>欲使徐甲之尸必起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377595_comment'></div>蔡经之骨重生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377595_comment'></div>仰嘉音而背若负山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377595_comment'></div>承厚旨而身如有翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377595_comment'></div>既容托迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377595_comment'></div>窃敢兴言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377595_comment'></div>某动不知机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377595_comment'></div>进惟招毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377595_comment'></div>忌王隐之名者虞豫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377595_comment'></div>暴苏秦之过者张仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377595_comment'></div>群居不出一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377595_comment'></div>彼则谓某矜才傲物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377595_comment'></div>痛饮不逾三爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377595_comment'></div>彼则谓某恃酒凌人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377595_comment'></div>何争名竞利之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377595_comment'></div>有蠹节食苗之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377595_comment'></div>苟非令君侧耳于车上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377595_comment'></div>中郎注目于亭间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377595_comment'></div>则随赵轭以长鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377595_comment'></div>与吴椽而共朽者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377595_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1377595_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3f35d10291c74c5a9bc2230bdc1942d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3f35d10291c74c5a9bc2230bdc1942d2");'><span id='3f35d10291c74c5a9bc2230bdc1942d2_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　朝廷下诏征四处士任谏官，韦遵居其一，诏下之日，韦某去世，作文予以讽刺。作品：代韦征君逊官疏。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_38066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄南城韦逸人</a><span class='authorDate'>（861年）</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（一作向）</span>豪<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作家）</span>家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38066'>美人晓折露沾袖，公子醉时香满车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38066'>万里丹青传不得，二年风雨恨无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38066'>羡他南涧高眠客，春去春来任物华。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38066'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38066_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c4d66d125ec7466489fbc8ac1ac2d8be_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c4d66d125ec7466489fbc8ac1ac2d8be");'><span id='c4d66d125ec7466489fbc8ac1ac2d8be_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=862')">861-862年</a>，29-30岁</div><div id='c4d66d125ec7466489fbc8ac1ac2d8be' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=861&endYear=861')">861年</a>　在长安。作品：拾甲子年事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年5月</a>　春试落第，看人变化，卧病在床，病中作疏文请皇上收回成命。作品：请追癸巳日诏疏。<div id='poem_1377584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请追癸已日诏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377584")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377584'>岁贡贱臣隐。既以文不得意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377584_comment'></div>且抱犬马之疾于长安。夏五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377584_comment'></div>京畿旱。癸已日闻诏大京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377584_comment'></div>用器水炉香蒲萧绛幡辈。致于坊市外门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377584_comment'></div>将以用旧法而召甘雨也。臣踊起病榻间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377584_comment'></div>以为明天子忧人。虽舜禹不如是之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377584_comment'></div>幸甚幸甚。臣又闻水旱与天地同出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377584_comment'></div>苟时或然。不可以仓卒除去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377584_comment'></div>今秦地旱已踰月矣。而陛下祷祠亦已频矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377584_comment'></div>天之高。地之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377584_comment'></div>五岳之绵亘。四渎之宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377584_comment'></div>陛下命百执事启祈外。何常不以心祝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377584_comment'></div>虽茎槁苗乾。而百姓不怨嗟者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377584_comment'></div>其感陛下之诚深也。今以蒲萧辈为请者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377584_comment'></div>岂陛下谓其能灵于岳渎者乎。夫岳渎视陛下之公辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377584_comment'></div>列陛下之土田。苟陛下忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377584_comment'></div>则岳渎亦宜忧矣。受祭据封者尚未能为陛下出力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377584_comment'></div>彼蒲萧辈复何足以动天。臣为陛下不取也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377584_comment'></div>臣又闻天之有雨泽。犹陛下之有渥恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377584_comment'></div>雨泽可以委曲干之。则陛下渥恩亦可以委曲干之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377584_comment'></div>臣闻天子有左右史。将所以记事记言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377584_comment'></div>然后付太史氏。臣必恐其得以容易编牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377584_comment'></div>今冒死请追癸已日诏。苟若陛下法十六圣之教训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377584_comment'></div>虽五种栖野。而百姓不暇掇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377584_comment'></div>岂蒲萧辈之所及乎哉。昔殷汤之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377584_comment'></div>民不以旱为灾。仁圣之君在上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377584_comment'></div>今旱未及殷代。而陛下忧已过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377584_comment'></div>臣谨因旱以质万姓。俾其知陛下心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377584_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1377584_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=862&endYear=862')">862年</a>　三举未第，作诗抒惶恐困苦之请。作品：投所思。<div id='poem_37895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377590_comment'></div>应倦施功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377590_comment'></div>忍随翔鸟之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377590_comment'></div>更望不龟之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377590_comment'></div>某沧州舍钓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377590_comment'></div>紫陌迷尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377590_comment'></div>徒欲信书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377590_comment'></div>不能知命。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377590_comment'></div>不惟长夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377590_comment'></div>魏舒对策。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377590_comment'></div>早避风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377590_comment'></div>敢因诱善之初。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377590_comment'></div>则数升泾水之泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377590_comment'></div>永依清济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377590_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1377590_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解武丁梦</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377620")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377620'>商之道削也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377620_comment'></div>武丁嗣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377620_comment'></div>且惧祖宗所传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377620_comment'></div>坏于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377620_comment'></div>祈于人则无以为质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377620_comment'></div>祷于家则不知天之历数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377620_comment'></div>厥有左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377620_comment'></div>民心不归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377620_comment'></div>然后念胥靡之可升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377620_comment'></div>且欲致于非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377620_comment'></div>而出于不测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377620_comment'></div>乃用假梦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1377620", 1377620, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>徵象</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377620_comment'></div>以活商命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377620_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377620_comment'></div>历数将去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377620_comment'></div>人心将解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377620_comment'></div>说复安能维之者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377620_comment'></div>武丁以下民之畏天命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377620_comment'></div>故设权以复之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377620_comment'></div>唯圣能神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377620_comment'></div>何梦之有。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1377620_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1377637' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377637' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377637?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秦始皇意</a><span class='authorDate'>（862年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377637")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377637_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377637'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377637'>秦法之于典坟。其酷也甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377637_comment'></div>由天文术数者。则不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377637_comment'></div>而易复从而免。噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377637_comment'></div>术数者未易知。而秦是以全易者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377637_comment'></div>其有旨哉。夫易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377637_comment'></div>肇于羲皇。演于姬昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377637_comment'></div>申于素王。其为书则百家九流之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377637_comment'></div>其造作者则百王之祖。其理则上下天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377637_comment'></div>出没鬼神。有春秋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377637_comment'></div>有诗书礼乐焉。开辟以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377637_comment'></div>举一物而言皆贯之。秦始皇通三圣之妙键。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377637_comment'></div>□故假术以言。亦将欲□圣人之旨乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377637_comment'></div>以是亹亹无道。而至灭亡者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377637_comment'></div>岂天下欲秦见造化之心乎。呜乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377637_comment'></div>言之于三代已前。秦则可以理遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377637_comment'></div>言之于战国之后。秦则为我罪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377637_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1377637_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='51be790a96fe4a32beee3785510a30d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("51be790a96fe4a32beee3785510a30d2");'><span id='51be790a96fe4a32beee3785510a30d2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=863&endYear=863')">863年</a>，31岁</div><div id='51be790a96fe4a32beee3785510a30d2' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春试落第，陆龟蒙春试落第欲东游，隐作文相送；与曹唐交往。作品：序陆生东游；；<div id='poem_1377608' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377608' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377608?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆生东游序</a><span class='authorDate'>（863年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377608")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377608_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377608'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377608'>余穷弃长安中二三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377608_comment'></div>时时于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1377608", 1377608, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>游骋</span>间面人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377608_comment'></div>未尝决胸臆事真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377608_comment'></div>自谓是非颠倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377608_comment'></div>不复得见其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377608_comment'></div>一年遇生于靖安里中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377608_comment'></div>相其吐气出词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377608_comment'></div>落落有正人风骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377608_comment'></div>余既急于近已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377608_comment'></div>而生亦以节槩见多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377608_comment'></div>自是出处游息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377608_comment'></div>不复狎他人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377608_comment'></div>虽患难厄穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377608_comment'></div>毁誉进退得丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377608_comment'></div>未尝不同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377608_comment'></div>有时因事慷慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377608_comment'></div>发涕泣相感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377608_comment'></div>以为读书不逢韩吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377608_comment'></div>作人不识阳先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377608_comment'></div>信吾徒之弊也宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377608_comment'></div>后一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377608_comment'></div>俱以所为道请于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377608_comment'></div>既不能以偷妄相梯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377608_comment'></div>又不能挟附相进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377608_comment'></div>果于数百人中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377608_comment'></div>不得吏部侍郎意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377608_comment'></div>由是知余者吊余以色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377608_comment'></div>不知者咥余以声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377608_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1377608", 1377608, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>愧负</span>彷徨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377608_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1377608", 1377608, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>扑浣</span>无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377608_comment'></div>既三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377608_comment'></div>生以故东出邹鲁间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377608_comment'></div>虽下第之绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377608_comment'></div>与将别之绪相煎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377608_comment'></div>然邹鲁圣人之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377608_comment'></div>亦足以暖生之憔悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377608_comment'></div>夫圣人羁旅七十国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377608_comment'></div>以君臣父子道未昭塞天地间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377608_comment'></div>独栖栖耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377608_comment'></div>是圣人患乎教不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377608_comment'></div>而不患乎名不彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377608_comment'></div>设使其早率一城啸一旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377608_comment'></div>则周之一诸侯材具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377608_comment'></div>复安有今日功业乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377608_comment'></div>生圣人徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377608_comment'></div>不当以圣人道为利家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1377608", 1377608, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>染后</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377608_comment'></div>狭其所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377608_comment'></div>且为余整衣冠拜朝堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377608_comment'></div>酌其车服礼乐之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377608_comment'></div>升降揖逊之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377608_comment'></div>思量侯伯卿士中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377608_comment'></div>复有夫子罪人否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377608_comment'></div>还日以言极之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377608_comment'></div>去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377608_comment'></div>青门晓开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377608_comment'></div>无一器酒以浇恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377608_comment'></div>明天子在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377608_comment'></div>不敢哭以致怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377608_comment'></div>勉之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377608_comment'></div>行与不行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377608_comment'></div>在生道耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377608_comment'></div>第与不第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377608_comment'></div>其如生何。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1377608_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>寄居长安华严寺。作品：寄洪正师。华严寺。<div id='poem_38067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38067' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=866&endYear=866')">866年</a>　春试落第，看人变化；春，吴兴沈光进士及第后东归完婚，隐有诗相赠；新罗国十二岁少年崔致远入唐参加宾贡科考试，首选罗隐为师；约本年至明年，与皮日休交游。作品：送沈先辈归，送上嘉礼。<div id='poem_37986' class='_poem'><div /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377603'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377603_comment'></div>某伏以内揣荒芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377603_comment'></div>早乖投献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377603_comment'></div>近者某官曲传尊旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377603_comment'></div>伏蒙郎中赐及卷纸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377603_comment'></div>令写近诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377603_comment'></div>捧对优荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377603_comment'></div>莫知所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377603_comment'></div>某利非楚铁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377603_comment'></div>钝甚燕锥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377603_comment'></div>濩落危根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377603_comment'></div>低摧壮节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377603_comment'></div>藏豹之功夫不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377603_comment'></div>屠龙之事业愈疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377603_comment'></div>爰自南国辞耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377603_comment'></div>东堂奉贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377603_comment'></div>剑迷船畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377603_comment'></div>胶在柱间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377603_comment'></div>靡旗而何啻再奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377603_comment'></div>绕树而岂惟三匝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377603_comment'></div>所以骚人避热。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377603_comment'></div>不忘吹齑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377603_comment'></div>元客求闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377603_comment'></div>长忧盖酱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377603_comment'></div>姑息于舆台之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377603_comment'></div>殷勤于阍侍之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377603_comment'></div>而犹往往拒关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377603_comment'></div>时时毁椟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377603_comment'></div>岂谓郎中俯敦吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377603_comment'></div>欲堰颓波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377603_comment'></div>不惮客嘲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377603_comment'></div>先从隗始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377603_comment'></div>寓剡藤而下授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377603_comment'></div>指巴句以旁徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377603_comment'></div>荣异当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377603_comment'></div>事殊近俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377603_comment'></div>而况风流渐泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377603_comment'></div>翰墨难言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377603_comment'></div>别路万般。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377603_comment'></div>中堂千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377603_comment'></div>虽欲坏虞卿之屩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377603_comment'></div>讵肯动心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377603_comment'></div>哭羊陟之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377603_comment'></div>何尝留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377603_comment'></div>复安有对纷华而辍玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377603_comment'></div>叩寂寞以搜遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377603_comment'></div>因使斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377603_comment'></div>亦归清鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377603_comment'></div>揣厚旨而时犹可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377603_comment'></div>荷殊私而力欲不任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377603_comment'></div>宁惟元晏吟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377603_comment'></div>空增纸价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377603_comment'></div>兼冀武卿窥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377603_comment'></div>免逐灰寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377603_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1377603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年1月</a>　编次《谗书》，并自作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年</a>　春，作《丁亥岁作中元甲子》诗，表达沮丧和不平。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年</a>　夏，前晋阳崔县令饿死于道政里，感慨而作《吊崔县令》文。<div id='poem_1377681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吊崔县令</a><span class='authorDate'>（867年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377681")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377681'>丁亥年夏<span class='inlineComment2'>（咸通八年）</span>。前晋阳崔县令死于通政里客舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377681_comment'></div>殍也。余虽不识其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377681_comment'></div>且念其官不卑也。死亦命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377681_comment'></div>而竟以饿者。是必不为贪吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377681_comment'></div>为贪吏则不然。因作词以吊曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377681_comment'></div>南风热兮云蒸乾。缅饥魂兮愁郁盘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377681_comment'></div>莅晋阳兮俸薄。魂之廉兮无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1377681", 1377681, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>剽削</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377681_comment'></div>余辞以吊空。魂来亲兮无西东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377681_comment'></div>魂无山兮山之鬼夷叔。彼之生兮未尝足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377681_comment'></div>魂无野兮野之鬼陈仲。彼非其得兮一介不之共。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377681_comment'></div>魂邀留兮京师。上愉愉兮下怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377681_comment'></div>残败肉兮乞狗彘。舍此兮何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377681_comment'></div>量天地之广大兮。吾不得而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377681_comment'></div>鸡则走而鸢则飞。鸣蝉瘦而蝤蛴肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377681_comment'></div>何浊也则是。清也则非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377681_comment'></div>茫昧既不可以问兮。盘礡不可得而推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377681_comment'></div>恍吾怀以四顾兮。孰知夫天地之云为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377681_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1377681_comment'></div></div></div><br href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年10月</a>　冬十月，随计入京。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=868&endYear=868')">868年</a>　春试落第，此时隐之从兄弟罗虬、罗邺均在京应试，知贡举刘允章以虬交通中贵，为“芳林十哲”之一，鄙其为人而黜落之，虬与隐、邺并称“三罗”；作品：寄袁皓侍御。<div id='poem_38072' class='_poem'><div onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1377610", 1377610, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>调膳</span>于江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377610_comment'></div>不随岁贡。又一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377610_comment'></div>朝廷以彭门就辟。刀机犹湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377610_comment'></div>诏吾辈不宜求试。然文章之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377610_comment'></div>不为举场也明矣。盖君子有其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377610_comment'></div>则执大柄以定是非。无其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377610_comment'></div>则著私书而疏善恶。斯所以警当世而诫将来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377610_comment'></div>自扬孟以下。何尝以名为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377610_comment'></div>而又念文皇帝致理之初。法制悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377610_comment'></div>必不以虮虱痒痛。遂偃斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377610_comment'></div>今年谏官有言。果动天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377610_comment'></div>所以不废谗书也。不亦宜乎。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=875')">874-875年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='ad471e041ffd4078ba9e06cf0d4f75ea' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=874')">874年</a>　北上长安再谋贡举，有诗寄虔州薛大夫；本年十月，郑畋入相，隐投诗拜谒，约在本年或明年，郑畋及其女皆欣赏罗隐诗，郑女甚至愿为隐妻，终因隐貌陋而破灭。<div id='poem_38071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄虔州薛大夫</a><span class='authorDate'>（874年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38071")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38071'>祝融峰下别，三载梦魂劳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=874')">874年</a>　本年冬至下年春试前，作启投李蔚。作品：投永宁李相公启。<div id='poem_1377591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377591?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投永宁李相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（874年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377591")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377591_comment'></div>某于今月三十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377591_comment'></div>获遂起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377591_comment'></div>伏以黄闼尊崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377591_comment'></div>虽容展敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377591_comment'></div>白衣卑贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377591_comment'></div>不敢兴言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377591_comment'></div>今则辄于陨穫之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377591_comment'></div>聊举證明之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377591_comment'></div>晋代则司空试剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377591_comment'></div>汉朝则丞相问牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377591_comment'></div>彼或以顽滞幽姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377591_comment'></div>或以疲驽下乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377591_comment'></div>犹能动摇至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377591_comment'></div>感达深仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377591_comment'></div>而况生禀五常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377591_comment'></div>早知恩义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377591_comment'></div>迹居十等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377591_comment'></div>不至舆台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377591_comment'></div>伏思癸卯年中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377591_comment'></div>维扬城畔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377591_comment'></div>谢傅裂土疆之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377591_comment'></div>羊公分节制之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377591_comment'></div>珠履玳簪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377591_comment'></div>朝盈望府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377591_comment'></div>鸡香豸角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377591_comment'></div>暮出行台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377591_comment'></div>转输则万井鱼盐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377591_comment'></div>统御则九州侯伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377591_comment'></div>当时务重难之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377591_comment'></div>是筹谋闲暇之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377591_comment'></div>南国佳辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377591_comment'></div>长闻赋咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377591_comment'></div>东山胜赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377591_comment'></div>屡见篇题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377591_comment'></div>为教化之笙镛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377591_comment'></div>作经纶之彩绘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377591_comment'></div>所以汉阳计吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377591_comment'></div>得诣军门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377591_comment'></div>厌次狂生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377591_comment'></div>叨蒙客礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377591_comment'></div>悯之以转蓬之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377591_comment'></div>安之以负米之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377591_comment'></div>进趋获奉于麾幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377591_comment'></div>俸入仍资于甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377591_comment'></div>其后何武捧诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377591_comment'></div>平阳趣装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377591_comment'></div>参佐廨中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377591_comment'></div>方虞浪迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377591_comment'></div>新城埭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377591_comment'></div>忽受温言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377591_comment'></div>嗟其未了之身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377591_comment'></div>勉以难迁之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377591_comment'></div>且怜色目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377591_comment'></div>犹可发扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377591_comment'></div>某是以不揣狂愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377591_comment'></div>重萌躁妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377591_comment'></div>出则祝赵衰之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377591_comment'></div>永冀流暄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377591_comment'></div>入则祷傅说之星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377591_comment'></div>惟希<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1377591", 1377591, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>借耀</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377591_comment'></div>今者风雨得生成之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377591_comment'></div>炉锤升鼓铸之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1377591_comment'></div>郭令军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1377591_comment'></div>潜抽妓乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1377591_comment'></div>崔宁城外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1377591_comment'></div>暗毁池台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1377591_comment'></div>登庸之时序未遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1377591_comment'></div>反旆之镃基已兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1377591_comment'></div>若某者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1377591_comment'></div>族惟单绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1377591_comment'></div>艺即中流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1377591_comment'></div>旋以佩服殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1377591_comment'></div>缄藏厚旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1377591_comment'></div>假昆虫而禀信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1377591_comment'></div>指簪履以输怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1377591_comment'></div>窃以浪逼龙津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1377591_comment'></div>风催律管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1377591_comment'></div>鱼皆五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1377591_comment'></div>禽必九苞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1377591_comment'></div>扬锦鬐彩羽之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1377591_comment'></div>俟启蛰吹葭之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1377591_comment'></div>独某行迷要路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1377591_comment'></div>坐守穷株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1377591_comment'></div>九品班资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1377591_comment'></div>略非亲旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1377591_comment'></div>六街车马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1377591_comment'></div>莫接声尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1377591_comment'></div>扪心而一寸寒灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1377591_comment'></div>泣泪而万行清血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1377591_comment'></div>良时易失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1377591_comment'></div>司马迁犹是再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1377591_comment'></div>知已难逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1377591_comment'></div>越石父于焉感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1377591_comment'></div>相公傥或俯回衡柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1377591_comment'></div>曲赐褒称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1377591_comment'></div>虽朽蠹不彫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1377591_comment'></div>则推常理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1377591_comment'></div>而孤寒无命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1377591_comment'></div>祇系洪钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1377591_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1377591_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=874')">874年</a>　本年冬末寄诗裴德符急求援引。作品：冬暮寄裴郎中。<div id='poem_38170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冬暮寄裴郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（874年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38170")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38170'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38170'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_38170", 38170, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>晓发</span>星星入镜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作鬓）</span>宜，早年容易近年悲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38170'>敢言得事时将晚，只恐酬恩日渐迟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38170'>南国倾心应望速，东堂开口欲从谁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38170'>仙郎旧有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_38170", 38170, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>黄金约</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_38170", 38170, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>沥胆隳肝</span>更<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_38170", 38170, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>祷祈</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38170_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38170'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=874')">874年</a>　作启投刑部尚书郑从谠。作品：投郑尚书启。<div id='poem_1377602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投郑尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（874年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377602")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377602'>某启。某前月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377602_comment'></div>辄以所为谗书一通。贡于客次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377602_comment'></div>尚书俯怜羁旅。遽赐沾濡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377602_comment'></div>既受厚恩。则宜前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377602_comment'></div>然而疆境有牵于感慨。风烟或轸于追思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377602_comment'></div>所以公子亭边。重嘘懦气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377602_comment'></div>侯嬴关畔。再转危肠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377602_comment'></div>何昔时有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1377602", 1377602, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>殉义</span>之人。而今日无死恩之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377602_comment'></div>辄复更弹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1377602", 1377602, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>冯铗</span>。上指膺门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377602_comment'></div>某也江左孤根。关中滞气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377602_comment'></div>强学早亡其皮骨。趋时久困于风尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377602_comment'></div>福星不照于命宫。旅火但焚其生计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377602_comment'></div>徘徊末路。惆怅危途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377602_comment'></div>览八行之诏书。空仰圣人在上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377602_comment'></div>咏五言之章句。未知游子何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377602_comment'></div>兴言而几至销魂。反袂而自然流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377602_comment'></div>尚书蕴稷契皋夔之事业。负卿轲迁固之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377602_comment'></div>入则藻镜冰壶。品量人物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377602_comment'></div>出则油幢瑞节。控御山河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377602_comment'></div>固已藏雷于伺蛰之时。待梦于驱羊之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377602_comment'></div>苟有一物未登其所。一夫不遂其怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377602_comment'></div>亦宜上下聪明。旁徨悯恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377602_comment'></div>傥或王衍之雌黄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1377602", 1377602, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>借润</span>。仲尼之日月回光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377602_comment'></div>则其人也。三千里之别离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377602_comment'></div>免为虚滞。十五年之勤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377602_comment'></div>永有所归。发自门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377602_comment'></div>百生知感。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377602_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1377602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年</a>　春试落第，章碣、黄滔亦本年落第，与黄滔之交盖始于此；春二月，投裴坦谋职位解决生计问题，未果。作品：投盐铁裴郎中启。<div id='poem_1377598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投盐铁裴郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（875年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377598")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377598'>某启。某闻大道五千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377598_comment'></div>所制者莫先于躁。浮生七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377598_comment'></div>所伤者莫甚于情。某所以反袂兴嗟<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作怀）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377598_comment'></div>支颐浩叹。顾两端而若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377598_comment'></div>持万绪以奚归。爰念龆年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377598_comment'></div>即偕时辈。胸中马骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377598_comment'></div>握内<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1377598", 1377598, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>蛇灵</span>。入公孙龙之关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377598_comment'></div>不惟逞辨。叱东方朔之御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377598_comment'></div>且欲献书。其后濩落单门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377598_comment'></div>蹉跎薄命。路穷鬼谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377598_comment'></div>天夺人谋。营生则饱少于饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377598_comment'></div>求试则落多于上。东经海峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377598_comment'></div>受下馆于诸侯。西出剑门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377598_comment'></div>泣危途于丞相。光景但销于杯酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377598_comment'></div>货财不入于橐装。传书而黄耳增劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377598_comment'></div>久客而黑貂兼敝。间者郎中丹青演润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377598_comment'></div>咳唾成音。荐光逸之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377598_comment'></div>以地寒为累。举仲宣之赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377598_comment'></div>以体弱见遗。既兴奔北之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377598_comment'></div>因指在东之念。江夏则铺名池口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377598_comment'></div>毗陵则堰号铜墩。皆有主张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377598_comment'></div>以生盐米。郎中倘或言泉晚浃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377598_comment'></div>未忘淘洒之功。谭柄时回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377598_comment'></div>别借齿牙之助<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作便）</span>。俾得内资柔滑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377598_comment'></div>外救困穷。然后驱淮阴入赵之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377598_comment'></div>更谋背水。整秦将渡河之卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377598_comment'></div>重议焚舟。目祷心祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377598_comment'></div>言狂意迫。其馀罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377598_comment'></div>不敢逭逃。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377598_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1377598_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年</a>　送李景温分司东都，有诗。作品：送李右丞分司。<div id='poem_37984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送李右丞分司<span class='inlineComment2'>（一本题下有东城二字）</span></a><span /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37984'>分漕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作左）</span>省曾批敕，中台肯避权。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37984'>所悲时渐薄，共贺道由<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=877&endYear=877')">877年</a>　在长安春雪中，与李洞等送别沈光全家赴福建幕。作品：送沈光侍御赴职闽中。<div id='poem_37987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=877&endYear=877')">877年3月2日</a>　三月二日，在长安以《谗书》一通行卷韦蟾，随后作启上韦蟾，以谋一职。作品：投前夏口韦尚书启。<div id='poem_1377589' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377589' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377589?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投前夏口韦尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（877年3月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377589'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377589'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377589_comment'></div>某今月二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377589_comment'></div>辄以近文一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377589_comment'></div>上凭阍侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377589_comment'></div>辞违既久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377589_comment'></div>僭越是虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377589_comment'></div>勒蹇步以戴恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377589_comment'></div>舍医门而奚适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377589_comment'></div>伏念随计渚宫之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377589_comment'></div>求闻汉浦之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377589_comment'></div>王俭望高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377589_comment'></div>芙蓉比幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377589_comment'></div>陈琳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1377589", 1377589, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>笔健</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377589_comment'></div>玳瑁为簪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377589_comment'></div>因矜窥豹之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377589_comment'></div>遂窃登龙之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377589_comment'></div>习池侍宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377589_comment'></div>岘岭从游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377589_comment'></div>许之以向者为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377589_comment'></div>颇胜张诩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377589_comment'></div>戒之以偶然成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377589_comment'></div>恐似李滂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377589_comment'></div>其后岁月煎熬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377589_comment'></div>轮蹄顽秃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377589_comment'></div>仅逾十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377589_comment'></div>幸免一鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377589_comment'></div>角羸而只有困时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377589_comment'></div>矢尽而未知降处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377589_comment'></div>间者尚书理兵夏汭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377589_comment'></div>栽柳武昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377589_comment'></div>文聘江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377589_comment'></div>粗资吟玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377589_comment'></div>费祎栏槛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377589_comment'></div>聊奉登临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377589_comment'></div>某比时尝驻征挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377589_comment'></div>仰趋画戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377589_comment'></div>方知叩洪钟而待教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377589_comment'></div>指坠履以明恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377589_comment'></div>而疾恙所牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377589_comment'></div>依投不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377589_comment'></div>伏枕而初惭数蹇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377589_comment'></div>扬帆而竟叹途穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377589_comment'></div>今则颍水政成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377589_comment'></div>旋为故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377589_comment'></div>中台位阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377589_comment'></div>已副急徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377589_comment'></div>风云将骋于康衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377589_comment'></div>神鬼肯论于宣室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377589_comment'></div>辄预提勃帚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377589_comment'></div>先立邱墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377589_comment'></div>虽哲匠抡材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377589_comment'></div>固须良木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377589_comment'></div>而洪钟许叩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377589_comment'></div>岂独兼金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377589_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1377589_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>　作书答贺兰友人质疑。作品：答贺兰友书。<div id='poem_1377587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答贺兰友书</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377587")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377587'>前者吾子不以仆之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>暗钝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377587_comment'></div>猥垂教示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377587_comment'></div>大相开发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377587_comment'></div>若非许与深至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377587_comment'></div>谁肯如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377587_comment'></div>甚善甚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377587_comment'></div>然其所道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377587_comment'></div>正中仆尝所自病者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377587_comment'></div>仆少而羁窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377587_comment'></div>自出山二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377587_comment'></div>所向摧沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377587_comment'></div>未尝有一得幸于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377587_comment'></div>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>同进</span>者忌仆之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377587_comment'></div>同志者忌仆之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377587_comment'></div>无有不如吾子之所诲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377587_comment'></div>然仆之所学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377587_comment'></div>不徒以竞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>科级</span>于今之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377587_comment'></div>盖将以窥昔贤之行止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377587_comment'></div>望作者之堂奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377587_comment'></div>期以方寸广圣人之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377587_comment'></div>可则垂于后代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377587_comment'></div>不可则庶几致身于无愧之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377587_comment'></div>宁复虞时人之罪仆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377587_comment'></div>与夫礼貌之于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377587_comment'></div>去就流俗不可以不时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377587_comment'></div>其进于秉笔立言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377587_comment'></div>扶植教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377587_comment'></div>当使前无所避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377587_comment'></div>后无所逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377587_comment'></div>岂以吾道沈浮于流俗者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377587_comment'></div>仲尼之于春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377587_comment'></div>惧之者乱臣贼子耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377587_comment'></div>未闻有不乱不贼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377587_comment'></div>疑仲尼于笔削之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377587_comment'></div>况仆求试京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377587_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>随波</span>而上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377587_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>逐队</span>而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377587_comment'></div>亦有年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377587_comment'></div>家在江表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377587_comment'></div>岁一<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>宁觐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377587_comment'></div>旨甘所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377587_comment'></div>桂玉之困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377587_comment'></div>何尝不以事力干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377587_comment'></div>苟利其出处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377587_comment'></div>则僶俛从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377587_comment'></div>亦人之常情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377587_comment'></div>在不枉其道而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377587_comment'></div>道苟不枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377587_comment'></div>以之流离可乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377587_comment'></div>冠衣不能移人之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377587_comment'></div>顾所履何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377587_comment'></div>言不忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377587_comment'></div>行不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377587_comment'></div>谓之君子可乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377587_comment'></div>言忠而行信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377587_comment'></div>谓之小人可乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377587_comment'></div>吾子视仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377587_comment'></div>复苟合于不信不忠者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377587_comment'></div>非仆之不可苟合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377587_comment'></div>道义之人皆不合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377587_comment'></div>而受性<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>介僻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377587_comment'></div>不能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1377587", 1377587, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>方圆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377587_comment'></div>既不与人合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1377587_comment'></div>而又视之如仇雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1377587_comment'></div>以是仆遂有狭而不容之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1377587_comment'></div>吾子果复发言及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1377587_comment'></div>是不以众人见待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1377587_comment'></div>而今而后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1377587_comment'></div>敢不安其所自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1377587_comment'></div>一科一级多难也有如是哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1377587_comment'></div>彼山也水也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1377587_comment'></div>性之所适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1377587_comment'></div>而眷眷不去者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1377587_comment'></div>以圣明之代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1377587_comment'></div>文物之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1377587_comment'></div>又安可以前所忌者移仆初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1377587_comment'></div>苟不得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1377587_comment'></div>仆亦自有所处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1377587_comment'></div>大凡内无所疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1377587_comment'></div>外无所愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1377587_comment'></div>则在乎命也天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1377587_comment'></div>焉在仆与时人乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1377587_comment'></div>惟吾子勿惮相规之数也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1377587_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>　作启感谢崔舍人去年对自己的推荐，感谢之余，决心东归。作品：谢崔舍人启。<div id='poem_1377593' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377593' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377593?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢崔舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377593")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377593_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377593'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377593'>某启。某镂冰伎短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377593_comment'></div>缘木计疏。去年舍人俯念穷迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377593_comment'></div>猥垂慰荐。竟以梁危易折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377593_comment'></div>气俗难医。负麈尾之高谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377593_comment'></div>困龙津之骇浪。虽怀感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377593_comment'></div>长抱忧惭。今月八日见某官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377593_comment'></div>伏知德水回波。重沾涸鲋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377593_comment'></div>灵丹减粒。已救伤蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377593_comment'></div>当谷莺刷羽之秋。是海燕窥梁之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377593_comment'></div>岂谓舍人未容祈祷。遽赐保明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377593_comment'></div>树立孤株。栽培弱蔓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377593_comment'></div>跪听而泪沾胸臆。仰承而背负邱山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377593_comment'></div>而况俗渐轻讹。时交势利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377593_comment'></div>或朝游夕处。或贵族华宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377593_comment'></div>至于取事之时。与能之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377593_comment'></div>犹须必成桃李。方许扶持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377593_comment'></div>若某者。迹未及萧阶<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作斋）</span>陈榻之严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377593_comment'></div>目未睹巢阁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1377593", 1377593, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>栖梧</span>之瑞。门寒于光逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377593_comment'></div>命薄于黔娄。纵饶委曲所私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377593_comment'></div>其奈纤毫无取。必舍人知其杀青废业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377593_comment'></div>二纪于兹。垂白倚门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377593_comment'></div>一生禺望。乃施阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377593_comment'></div>以慰归心。言念徘徊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377593_comment'></div>不知所处。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377593_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1377593_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='82593fd7250844e99800a2608dd4b9ee_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("82593fd7250844e99800a2608dd4b9ee");'><span id='82593fd7250844e99800a2608dd4b9ee_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>，46岁</div><div id='82593fd7250844e99800a2608dd4b9ee' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋居于道德里。作品：西京道德里。<div id='poem_37885' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37885' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37885?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西京道德里</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37885")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37885_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_37885'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(854, "poem_allusion_37885")'>吟同楚执圭</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5378, "poem_allusion_37885")'>一枝丹桂</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_37885_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37885'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37885'>秦树团团夕结阴，此中庄舄动悲吟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37885'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5378, "poem_sentence_1_37885")'>一枝丹桂</span>未入手，万里苍波长负心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37885'>老去渐知时态薄，愁来唯愿酒杯深。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37885'>七雄三杰今何在，休为闲人泪满襟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37885_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37885'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37885_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长安城南。作品：城南杂感。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长安。作品：长安秋夜。<div id='poem_37842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长安秋夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37842")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37842_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_37842'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5378, "poem_allusion_37842")'>一枝仙桂</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_37842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37842'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37842'>远闻天子似羲皇，偶舍渔乡入帝乡。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37842'>五等列侯无故旧，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5378, "poem_sentence_1_37842")'>一枝仙桂</span>有风霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37842'>灯欹短焰烧离鬓，漏转寒更滴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_37842", 37842, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>旅肠</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37842'>归计未知身已老，九衢双阙夜苍苍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37842'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，在长安送李某出任汝州刺史。作品：送汝州李中丞十二韵。<div id='poem_38167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送汝州李中丞十二韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38167")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_38167_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_38167'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(325, "poem_allusion_38167")'>白梃</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3146, "poem_allusion_38167")'>福星</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4248, "poem_allusion_38167")'>黄巾</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_38167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38167'>群盗方为梗，分符奏未宁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38167'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4248, "poem_sentence_1_38167")'>黄巾</span>攻郡邑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(325, "poem_sentence_1_38167")'>白梃</span>掠生灵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38167'>尘土周畿暗，疮痍汝水腥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38167'>一凶虽剪灭，数县尚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_38167", 38167, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>凋零</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38167'>理必资<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_38167", 38167, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>宽猛</span>，谋须藉典刑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_38167'>与能才物论，慎选忽天庭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_38167'>官品尊台秩，山河拥<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3146, "poem_sentence_6_38167")'>福星</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_38167'>虎知应去境，牛在肯全形。<div id='poem_sentence_7_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_38167'>旧政穷人瘼，新衔展武经。<div id='poem_sentence_8_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_38167'>关防秋草白，城壁晚峰青。<div id='poem_sentence_9_38167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
大荔
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='49eb525d6d2c473a90cb74237d186bef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49eb525d6d2c473a90cb74237d186bef");'><span id='49eb525d6d2c473a90cb74237d186bef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>，28岁</div><div id='49eb525d6d2c473a90cb74237d186bef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=860&endYear=860')">860年</a>　干谒杨汉公，未果。作品：投同州杨尚书启。<div id='poem_1377600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投同州杨尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（860年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377600")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377600'>某启。某闻足历屠门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377600_comment'></div>尚能大嚼。力疲吴坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377600_comment'></div>亦解长鸣。而况睹棠阴教化之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377600_comment'></div>入黍谷暄和之景。苟不能自提由瑟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377600_comment'></div>直犯孔墙。则其人生为无益之徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377600_comment'></div>死作无知之鬼。某谯乡贱族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377600_comment'></div>钓濑遗氓。钜下二卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377600_comment'></div>素非朋执。于陵一叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377600_comment'></div>或与交游。偶然蒙郭泰之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377600_comment'></div>歘尔厉苏秦之志。遂得麦漂风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377600_comment'></div>门长蒿莱。旋慕题桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377600_comment'></div>因吟入洛。三秋旅寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377600_comment'></div>身居计吏之先。万里徒行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377600_comment'></div>家匪大夫之后。孰谓九街浪阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377600_comment'></div>双阙云浮。姜维之胆有破时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377600_comment'></div>李阳之拳无下处。由是潜伤鲋辙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377600_comment'></div>暗泣牛衣。贾谊长缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377600_comment'></div>虽犹自运。张仪健舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377600_comment'></div>亦拟何为。前窥而四海清平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377600_comment'></div>内顾而一身流落。辄复徘徊郑驿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377600_comment'></div>睥睨秦医。敢言画虎之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377600_comment'></div>但有伤蛇之望。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377600_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1377600_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永济

class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377601")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377601'>某启。某闻歌者不系声音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377601_comment'></div>惟思中节。言者不期枝叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377601_comment'></div>所贵达情。苟抑扬之理或差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377601_comment'></div>则流<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作荒）</span>诞之辞亦弃。而况委病<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1377601", 1377601, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>鹊门</span>之下<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作外）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377601_comment'></div>窥光龙烛之前。上方于赵壹遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377601_comment'></div>下比于陆机荣显。虽倜傥不侔于二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377601_comment'></div>而辉华敢让于伊人。今则住踰负岳之蚊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377601_comment'></div>去切恋轩之马。辄复重将越调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377601_comment'></div>更唱燕台。以为京兆王章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377601_comment'></div>三冬有泪。淮阴韩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377601_comment'></div>一饭无门。惟忧委骨穷尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377601_comment'></div>敢望横戈要路。加以轻蹄逸轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377601_comment'></div>犹祈公子王孙。同窥万顷波澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377601_comment'></div>各有一时颜色。而某短袖难舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377601_comment'></div>危条易风。祷祠则天或未从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377601_comment'></div>号泣则人皆不吊。由是饰装增欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377601_comment'></div>览策兴嗟。指棨戟以凝神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377601_comment'></div>望炉锤之借便。虽琳琅梓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377601_comment'></div>尽归梁栋之间。而藻荇蘋蘩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377601_comment'></div>亦恋池亭之内。殷函轸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377601_comment'></div>刘纸悬缄。无言誓天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377601_comment'></div>有死铭德。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377601_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1377601_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div
