class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37825")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37825'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37825'>前年帝里望<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作从）</span>行尘，记得仙家第四人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37825'>泉暖旧谙龙偃息，露寒初见鹤精神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37825'>歌声上榻梁园晚，梦绕残钟汜水春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37825'>知有箧中编集在，只应从此是经纶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37825_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37825'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=864&endYear=864')">864年</a>　秋，辞别郑处诲南归。作品：辞宣武郑尚书启。<div id='poem_1377605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞宣武郑尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（864年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377605")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377605'>某启。某闻郑司农之东去绛纱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377605_comment'></div>感深吾道。谢记室之西辞朱邸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377605_comment'></div>恋切所知。虽定名之分则殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377605_comment'></div>而怀德之心不异。其有栖羸乐厩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377605_comment'></div>养病医门。海燕辞巢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377605_comment'></div>即摧萍影。林乌绕树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377605_comment'></div>忽轸蓬心。又安得下弃席于诗人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377605_comment'></div>感崩波于行客。某也风尘下物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377605_comment'></div>天地中材。光逸门寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377605_comment'></div>无因自进。扬雄口吃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377605_comment'></div>徒欲解嘲。属者尚书置驿恩宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377605_comment'></div>敦风志大。孔文举之干元礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377605_comment'></div>既忝登门。徐孺子之谒陈蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377605_comment'></div>俄蒙下榻。淹延馆宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377605_comment'></div>荏苒春秋。稻粱有异于他人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377605_comment'></div>觞豆时陪于上客。那言此际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377605_comment'></div>遽怆离声。背重德于邱山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377605_comment'></div>揖红尘于道路。缅怀今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377605_comment'></div>杳不胜情。加以贡部伤心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377605_comment'></div>名场落羽。兽因斗困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377605_comment'></div>羊以多亡。前瞻既倦于吹齑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377605_comment'></div>内顾徒悲于求剑。昔也来惭赋雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377605_comment'></div>谬称梁苑之游。今则去类乞师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377605_comment'></div>己抱秦庭之哭。倚征轮而怅望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377605_comment'></div>指断鞭以夷犹。尚书傥或仙客壶中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377605_comment'></div>旁均日月。山公启里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377605_comment'></div>别借篇题。无令一叶先秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377605_comment'></div>遂对满堂垂泣。舍此丹须九转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377605_comment'></div>桃指千年。天也何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377605_comment'></div>时乎不再。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377605_comment'></div></div><div -----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0cf178bc07cb4753a0efc237fbe39169_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0cf178bc07cb4753a0efc237fbe39169");'><span id='0cf178bc07cb4753a0efc237fbe39169_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=867&endYear=867')">867年</a>，35岁</div><div id='0cf178bc07cb4753a0efc237fbe39169' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏秋之际，赴东都洛阳干谒、取解，先以《谗书》行卷检校户部尚书、秘书监韦澳，随后作《投秘监韦尚书启》，《启》中提及自己本年已考了六次。作品：投秘书监韦尚书启。<div id='poem_1377596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投秘监韦尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（867年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377596")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377596'>某启。某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377596_comment'></div>以所著谗书一通。寓于阍吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377596_comment'></div>退量僭越。伏积忧惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377596_comment'></div>某闻樊子昭之处屠沽。发光辉于许邵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377596_comment'></div>郭林宗之游巩洛。振声价于符融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377596_comment'></div>其后物态乖讹。风流委败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377596_comment'></div>下有自媒之诮。上无相汲之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377596_comment'></div>某由是反袂兴怀。扪心注恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377596_comment'></div>又安得不属耳于舆人之论。倾怀于长者之谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377596_comment'></div>而尚书以盛名镇乎当时。以盛德传乎奕世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377596_comment'></div>不趑趄于阘茸。不浮泛于奸回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377596_comment'></div>动则致圣主而活苍生。以为己任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377596_comment'></div>静则导冲襟而养和气。以守家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377596_comment'></div>恭惟大朝。属在吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377596_comment'></div>若某者。燎薪就学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377596_comment'></div>掷楯攻文。一则以神气低凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377596_comment'></div>不足动王侯之瞻视。一则以家门寒贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377596_comment'></div>不足辱卿相之搜扬。十年索米于京都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377596_comment'></div>六举随波而上下。永言浮世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377596_comment'></div>堪比多岐。所以览嵇叔夜之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377596_comment'></div>则伏膺户外。读张季鹰之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377596_comment'></div>则大嚼窗间。长恐一旦月桂情衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377596_comment'></div>江蘋思起。不得揖兖国山庭之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377596_comment'></div>不得窥汉朝王佐之才。是以重拂尘衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377596_comment'></div>聊希藻鉴。傥尚书以孺子可教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377596_comment'></div>则随洛下之书生。傥尚书以斯人若狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377596_comment'></div>则访江东之钓叟。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1377596", 1377596, "Clauses/53/Comments/0")'>灵蓍</span>神蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377596_comment'></div>惟祷所从。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377596_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1377596_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，又先以《谗书》行卷东京太常寺房千里博士，随后作《上太常房博士启》投之。<div id='poem_1377597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太常房博士启</a><span class='authorDate'>（867年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377597")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377597'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377597_comment'></div>某前月二十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377597_comment'></div>以所著谗书一通上献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377597_comment'></div>近见某官某乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377597_comment'></div>伏承博士曲垂题品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377597_comment'></div>俯及孤危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377597_comment'></div>某闻孙阳以一顾之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377597_comment'></div>骐骥不为驽马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377597_comment'></div>宣父以一言之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377597_comment'></div>夷齐不作饿夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377597_comment'></div>苟吾道之未亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377597_comment'></div>谅斯人而何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377597_comment'></div>某也薪就学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377597_comment'></div>阅市成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377597_comment'></div>偶不自量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377597_comment'></div>因思妄动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377597_comment'></div>舍五湖之高蹈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377597_comment'></div>事九陌之穷游<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作途）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377597_comment'></div>为良工不度之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377597_comment'></div>为要路不容之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377597_comment'></div>所以嵇康奏乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377597_comment'></div>忿魑魅以争光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377597_comment'></div>刘子营生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377597_comment'></div>奈鬼神之相笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377597_comment'></div>那言不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377597_comment'></div>一至于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377597_comment'></div>恭惟咸通之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377597_comment'></div>大中之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377597_comment'></div>故荆南余正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377597_comment'></div>以博士为轩镜庖刀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377597_comment'></div>今渭北徐端公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377597_comment'></div>以博士为灵蓍神蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377597_comment'></div>但言薄技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377597_comment'></div>合在殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377597_comment'></div>其后某则困踬于龙津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377597_comment'></div>博士则徊翔于鹓侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377597_comment'></div>虽心祈目祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377597_comment'></div>不忘斯须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377597_comment'></div>而天上人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377597_comment'></div>凭谁讯问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377597_comment'></div>宁知此日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377597_comment'></div>属在明思<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作恩）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377597_comment'></div>岂一旅人之遭遇有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377597_comment'></div>而二作者之语言斯中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377597_comment'></div>永为负荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377597_comment'></div>适足忧惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377597_comment'></div>况复风讹俗败之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377597_comment'></div>辙乱旗奔之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377597_comment'></div>讲学则卫刀削树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377597_comment'></div>论文则嬴火烧人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377597_comment'></div>家家无相保之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377597_comment'></div>处处有自媒之口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377597_comment'></div>而博士独持大旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377597_comment'></div>高坐危城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377597_comment'></div>招既散之师徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377597_comment'></div>复已亡之土地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377597_comment'></div>顾兹隆替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377597_comment'></div>尤属尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377597_comment'></div>某也虽赋命以多奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377597_comment'></div>或因人而成事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377597_comment'></div>愿将所贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377597_comment'></div>以贺明时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377597_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1377597_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fbd0066edca44215b4c8b737d5775be5_label'><a href='javascript: -----title
合肥
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a1e71ab9ed1a43239986f180e8f5138f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1e71ab9ed1a43239986f180e8f5138f");'><span id='a1e71ab9ed1a43239986f180e8f5138f_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>约本年春，经庐州，游巢湖。作品：四顶山。姥山。巢县半汤池。<div id='poem_37855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37855?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_0_37855'>胜景天然别，精神入画图。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37855'>一山分四顶，三面瞰平湖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_37855_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_37936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37936?labeling=true' "poem_title_37936")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37936'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37936'>临塘古庙一神仙，绣幌花容色俨然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37936'>为逐朝云来此地，因随暮雨不归天。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37936'>眉分初月湖中鉴，香散馀风竹上烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37936'>借问邑人沈水事，已经秦汉几千年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37936'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37936_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
淮安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a58ed6124dab49dd8a1f25cf49beb714_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a58ed6124dab49dd8a1f25cf49beb714");'><span id='a58ed6124dab49dd8a1f25cf49beb714_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=868&endYear=868')">868年</a>，36岁</div><div id='a58ed6124dab49dd8a1f25cf49beb714' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=868&endYear=868')">868年</a>　庞勋叛军攻打泗州夺取淮口，唐将戴可师欲夺，结果大败，隐欲北上参加科举考试，至淮口，目睹惨况，作诗。作品：淮口军葬。<div id='poem_37793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>淮口军葬</a><span class='authorDate'>（868年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37793")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_37793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37793'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37793'>一阵孤军不复回，更无分别只荒堆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37793'>莫言赋分须如此，曾作文皇赤子来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37793_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37793'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_37793_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6995ef23703941dabd3727a933266dda_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6995ef23703941dabd3727a933266dda");'><span id='6995ef23703941dabd3727a933266dda_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>，37岁</div><div id='6995ef23703941dabd3727a933266dda' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=869&endYear=869')">869年</a>　春，在苏州杭州衢州一带活动，在衢州时，于刺史孙玉汝幕逗留数旬，颇受恩遇，东下至龙丘时有诗表感激。作品：龙丘东下却寄孙员外。<div id='poem_37861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙泉<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作丘）</span>东下却寄孙员外</a><span class='authorDate'>（869年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37861")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37861'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37861'>縠江东下几多程，每泊孤舟即有情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37861'>山色已随游子远，水纹犹认主人清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37861'>恩如海岳何时报，恨似烟花触处生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37861'>百尺风帆两行泪，不堪回首望峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37861_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37861'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37861_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c9873d26aa02499797033c935b2dc906_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9873d26aa02499797033c935b2dc906");'><span id='c9873d26aa02499797033c935b2dc906_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>，39岁</div><div id='c9873d26aa02499797033c935b2dc906' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　经衢州，此时衢州刺史孙玉汝已赴阙入京，隐有诗。作品：孙员外赴阙后重到三衢。<div id='poem_37866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37866'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37866'>远山高树思悠哉，重倚危楼尽一杯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37866'>谢守已随徵诏入，鲁儒犹逐断蓬来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37866_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37866'>地寒谩忆移暄手，时急方须济世才。<div -----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='21f2a214a2ee4ae4af6fc2c87ae727e7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("21f2a214a2ee4ae4af6fc2c87ae727e7");'><span id='21f2a214a2ee4ae4af6fc2c87ae727e7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=871')">870-871年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='21f2a214a2ee4ae4af6fc2c87ae727e7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=870&endYear=870')">870年</a>　冬，在长沙入于瑰湖南观察使幕，事笔砚。作品：投湖南于常侍启。<div id='poem_1377594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投湖南于常侍启</a><span class='authorDate'>（870年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377594")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377594'>某启。某闻淮王鍊迹于真仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377594_comment'></div>含灵尽去。邹衍移暄于寒谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377594_comment'></div>众卉皆芳。岂羽毛可从于霓旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377594_comment'></div>岂凋蘖尽关于葭律。盖以至道无遗于一物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377594_comment'></div>殊私必及于群生。某尝佩斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377594_comment'></div>请陈丹恳。间者豹藏不稳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377594_comment'></div>鱼跃无成。浼山公启事之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377594_comment'></div>累王衍雌黄之口。扪天莫及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377594_comment'></div>跼地兴惭。向浮世以伤怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377594_comment'></div>拊劳生而自喟。光阴不驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377594_comment'></div>齿发渐高。当家贫亲老之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377594_comment'></div>是失路亡羊之日。泪将欲尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377594_comment'></div>口不敢开。直以非汉代之簪裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377594_comment'></div>困晋朝之流品。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1377594", 1377594, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>物汇</span>虽逃于刍狗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377594_comment'></div>孤寒竟陷于虫沙。所以仰蟾桂之高高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377594_comment'></div>恐无仙骨。睹鱼鬐之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1377594", 1377594, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>敛敛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377594_comment'></div>忽有痴心。窃希常侍从来许与之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377594_comment'></div>作此改张之计。俾其七郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377594_comment'></div>与奏一官。致之于髯参短簿之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377594_comment'></div>责之以驽马铅刀之用。所冀内资骨肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377594_comment'></div>外罄筋骸。但系受恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377594_comment'></div>何须及第。必若终怜薄技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377594_comment'></div>尚悯前途。则科号三篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377594_comment'></div>判称六部。早尝留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377594_comment'></div>颇亦逼人。将今晨祷祝之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377594_comment'></div>为异日觊觎之路。情虽可恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377594_comment'></div>僭亦堪诛。对胶柱以轸怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377594_comment'></div>愿漆身而在此。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377594_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1377594_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　春在长沙幕；罗邺漂泊于潇湘，或曾与隐相聚。作品：湘中见进士乔诩。<div id='poem_38115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湘中见进士乔诩</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38115")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38115'>吴公台下别经秋，破虏城边暂驻留。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　途中有咏史诗。作品：览晋史张翰思吴中鲈鲙莼羹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年10月19日</a>　乘船顶风北上出长沙边界，作启谢于瑰。作品：谢湖南于常侍启。<div id='poem_1377606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢湖南于常侍启</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年10月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377606")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377606'>某启。某今月十九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377606_comment'></div>已至界首。回望旌棨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377606_comment'></div>涕泣不任。某庄栎粗疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377606_comment'></div>庾膏昏钝。不能量力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377606_comment'></div>尝欲干名。随贡部以悽惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377606_comment'></div>将邻十上。看时人之颜色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377606_comment'></div>岂止一朝。进则刺灭许都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377606_comment'></div>退则歌终汉垒。地虽至广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377606_comment'></div>人莫相容。凭执爨以无由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377606_comment'></div>假邻光而不得。常侍独于此际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377606_comment'></div>降以深仁。奏仇览之官资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377606_comment'></div>近陈遵之尺牍。福由无妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377606_comment'></div>荣亦何酬。近者以江表岁饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377606_comment'></div>吴中力困。旨甘既阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377606_comment'></div>晨夕萦怀。常侍不顾人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377606_comment'></div>将逾事例。给使府留州之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377606_comment'></div>代衡阳计岁之资。俾以东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377606_comment'></div>救其栖旅。蔡泽北游之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377606_comment'></div>瓶甑不存。陆生南返之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377606_comment'></div>橐装皆满。聊将自衒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377606_comment'></div>粗可讳穷。但以感切违梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377606_comment'></div>情深去鲁。辞画戟而心犹似醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377606_comment'></div>上孤舟而泪始如流。盖以非故旧之由缘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377606_comment'></div>无强近之慰荐。只因奖善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377606_comment'></div>便与致身。如某之孤贱者则多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377606_comment'></div>似某之遭逢者则少。以兹自誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377606_comment'></div>安可暂忘。今则尚有回期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377606_comment'></div>犹宽旅思。石尤风定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377606_comment'></div>桥口浪衰。展片席以高飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377606_comment'></div>指重湖而直过。地名北渚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377606_comment'></div>长牵楚客之心。水到东吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377606_comment'></div>敢忘湘江<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作波）</span>之色。谨启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377606_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1377606_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='28ee56a7ffbf46d5b2ac1269a98d55ed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28ee56a7ffbf46d5b2ac1269a98d55ed");'><span id='28ee56a7ffbf46d5b2ac1269a98d55ed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=873&endYear=873')">873年</a>，41岁</div><div id='28ee56a7ffbf46d5b2ac1269a98d55ed' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长沙，投湖南观察使王凝，再谋官职，未果，参加进士考试已八次。作品：投湖南王大夫启。<div id='poem_1377592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377592?labeling=true' "poem_title_1377592")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377592'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377592_comment'></div>某闻元亮苦贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377592_comment'></div>姑求彭泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377592_comment'></div>戴禺多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377592_comment'></div>遂乞海虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377592_comment'></div>苟物役之是牵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377592_comment'></div>亦人情而斯见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377592_comment'></div>某族惟单贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377592_comment'></div>品在下中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377592_comment'></div>三箧亡书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377592_comment'></div>幸无遗漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377592_comment'></div>一枝仙桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377592_comment'></div>尝欲觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377592_comment'></div>十年恸哭于秦庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377592_comment'></div>八举摧风于宋野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377592_comment'></div>近者以调甘轸虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377592_comment'></div>负米撄心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377592_comment'></div>毛义前贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377592_comment'></div>尚犹捧檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377592_comment'></div>鲰生何者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377592_comment'></div>焉可守株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377592_comment'></div>勒气马以徐回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377592_comment'></div>解藩羊而适愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377592_comment'></div>前使常侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377592_comment'></div>遽怜此志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377592_comment'></div>遂以奏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377592_comment'></div>藉俸入于衡阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377592_comment'></div>专表章于使府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377592_comment'></div>虽元瑜书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377592_comment'></div>不足愈风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377592_comment'></div>而处士衣裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377592_comment'></div>未尝换雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377592_comment'></div>斯亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1377592", 1377592, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>冤鸟</span>尚思于衔石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377592_comment'></div>愚公犹锐于移山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377592_comment'></div>寻遇大夫辍梦轩宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377592_comment'></div>吹暄楚峤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377592_comment'></div>手中扇在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377592_comment'></div>河必袁宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377592_comment'></div>天上才高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377592_comment'></div>宁惟公辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377592_comment'></div>间者龙门掌贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377592_comment'></div>马帐搜遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377592_comment'></div>泉客号咷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377592_comment'></div>只忧宝尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377592_comment'></div>地灵惆怅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377592_comment'></div>不觉山空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377592_comment'></div>而某适限徐兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377592_comment'></div>远留吴会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377592_comment'></div>不得少将鳞鬣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377592_comment'></div>侧望风雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377592_comment'></div>指函谷以驰诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377592_comment'></div>遥知气紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377592_comment'></div>上苏台而送目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377592_comment'></div>空羡河清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377592_comment'></div>今者辄奉危心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377592_comment'></div>来干画戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377592_comment'></div>大夫或俯回赵印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377592_comment'></div>下煦韩灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377592_comment'></div>更于茶药之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377592_comment'></div>重假勾留之便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377592_comment'></div>所冀犹縻禄食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377592_comment'></div>远救朝昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377592_comment'></div>迹稍免于屡空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1377592_comment'></div>心尚期于妄动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1377592_comment'></div>百生可卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1377592_comment'></div>式占郭泰之龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1377592_comment'></div>一字为褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1377592_comment'></div>全系宣尼之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1377592_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1377592_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作诗悼念于瑰。作品：春日忆湖南旧游寄卢校书。<div id='poem_37941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春日忆湖南旧游寄卢校书</a><span class='authorDate'>（873年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · -----title
岳阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1fe3b0730de24d17a206a1fd95883f41_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fe3b0730de24d17a206a1fd95883f41");'><span id='1fe3b0730de24d17a206a1fd95883f41_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=871&endYear=871')">871年</a>　阻风于洞庭、青草间，编次《湖南应用集》三卷，并作序。作品：湘南应用集。湘南应用集序。<div id='poem_1377612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湘南应用集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（871年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377612")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377612'>隐大中末即在贡籍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377612_comment'></div>命薄地卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377612_comment'></div>自己卯至于庚寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377612_comment'></div>一十二年看人变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377612_comment'></div>去年冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377612_comment'></div>河南公按察长沙郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377612_comment'></div>隐因请事笔砚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377612_comment'></div>以资甘旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377612_comment'></div>明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377612_comment'></div>隐得衡阳县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377612_comment'></div>时硖州卢侍御自龙城至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377612_comment'></div>右司张员外游曲江回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377612_comment'></div>皆谓隐不宜佐属邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377612_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377612_comment'></div>隐自卜也审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377612_comment'></div>江表一白丁耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377612_comment'></div>安有空将卷轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377612_comment'></div>与公相子弟争名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377612_comment'></div>幸而知非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377612_comment'></div>得以减过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377612_comment'></div>冬十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377612_comment'></div>乞假归觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377612_comment'></div>阻风于洞庭青草间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377612_comment'></div>因思湘南文书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377612_comment'></div>十不一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377612_comment'></div>盖以失落于马上军前故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377612_comment'></div>今分为三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377612_comment'></div>而举牒祠祭者亦与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377612_comment'></div>某月二十四日序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1377612_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='514786cbbda64264a6626463b6a80217_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("514786cbbda64264a6626463b6a80217");'><span id='514786cbbda64264a6626463b6a80217_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=873&endYear=873')">873年</a>，41岁</div><div id='514786cbbda64264a6626463b6a80217' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=873&endYear=873')">873年2月</a>　春二月，南下长沙，过岳阳，有诗。作品：早春巴陵道中。<div id='poem_37869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>早春巴陵道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（873年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37869")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37869'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37869'>远雪亭亭望未销，岳阳春浅似相饶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37869'>短芦冒土初生笋，高柳偷风已弄条。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37869_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37869'>波汎洞庭猵獭健，谷连荆楚鬼神妖。<div id='poem_sentence_4_37869'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37869_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='44c83edefff3414ea7d91fe1d5b9fe70_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("44c83edefff3414ea7d91fe1d5b9fe70");'><span id='44c83edefff3414ea7d91fe1d5b9fe70_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年</a>　曾游安陆，与徐砺相逢又相别。作品：安陆赠徐砺。<div id='poem_37867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安陆赠徐砺</a><span class='authorDate'>（875年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37867")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_37867_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_37867'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1463, "poem_allusion_37867")'>一榻依陈</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6340, id='poem_sentence_0_37867'>灵蛇桥下水声声，曾向桥边话别情。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37867'>一榻偶依陈太守，三<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作二）</span>年深忆<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6340, "poem_sentence_1_37867")'>祢先生</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37867'>尘欺鬓色非前事，火爇蓬根有去程。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37867'>还把馀杯重相劝，不堪秋色背郧城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_37867_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_37867'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_37867_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c3071158a539410ab806a1349f819ddb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c3071158a539410ab806a1349f819ddb");'><span id='c3071158a539410ab806a1349f819ddb_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，东下江州。作品：九江早秋。上江州陈员外。赠无相禅师。中元传。滕王阁。<div id='poem_37818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37818?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_37818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37818'>百岁几多日，四蹄无限程<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作尘）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37820'>旧班久望鹓晴翥，馀力犹闻虎夜浮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37820_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' -----title
潍坊
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c1e4246cf7c34c96a93db2e3745fd180_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1e4246cf7c34c96a93db2e3745fd180");'><span id='c1e4246cf7c34c96a93db2e3745fd180_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年</a>，44岁</div><div id='c1e4246cf7c34c96a93db2e3745fd180' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年6月</a>　六月赴青州诣军门向宋威上书。作品：与招讨宋将军书。<div id='poem_1377588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上招讨宋将军书</a><span class='authorDate'>（876年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377588")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377588'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377588'>朝廷以简陵九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377588_comment'></div>彭虺肆螫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377588_comment'></div>而东南一臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377588_comment'></div>为之枯耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377588_comment'></div>其后吴卒以狼山叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377588_comment'></div>则东西浙之筋力殆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377588_comment'></div>自尔天子不忍重困百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377588_comment'></div>由是官朱实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377588_comment'></div>爵诸葛爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377588_comment'></div>秩安文祏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377588_comment'></div>皆自盗而升<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1377588", 1377588, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>朝序</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377588_comment'></div>所以不幸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377588_comment'></div>江南水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377588_comment'></div>钟陵火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377588_comment'></div>沿淮饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377588_comment'></div>汴滑以东螟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377588_comment'></div>故无赖辈一食之不饱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377588_comment'></div>一衣之不覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377588_comment'></div>则磨寸铁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377588_comment'></div>梃白棒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377588_comment'></div>以望朝廷姑息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377588_comment'></div>而王仙芝尚君长等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377588_comment'></div>淩突我庐寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377588_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1377588", 1377588, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>燖剥</span>我梁宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377588_comment'></div>天子以虮虱痛痒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377588_comment'></div>不足搔爬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377588_comment'></div>因处分十二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377588_comment'></div>取将军为节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377588_comment'></div>非方镇之无帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377588_comment'></div>非朝廷之乏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377588_comment'></div>盖以将军跳出陇右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377588_comment'></div>不二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377588_comment'></div>三拥节旄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377588_comment'></div>谓将军必能知恩用命耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377588_comment'></div>今闻群盗已拔睢阳二城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377588_comment'></div>大梁亦版筑自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377588_comment'></div>彼之望将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377588_comment'></div>其犹沸之待沃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377588_comment'></div>压之待起也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377588_comment'></div>而将军朱轮大旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377588_comment'></div>优游东道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377588_comment'></div>不知朝廷以八十三州奉将军侍卫者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377588_comment'></div>抑将俾将军旦夕剪此草寇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377588_comment'></div>昔韩之医良而性啬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377588_comment'></div>故为人治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377588_comment'></div>未尝剔去根源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377588_comment'></div>所以延其疾而养其财也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377588_comment'></div>后有商于韩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377588_comment'></div>以疽见医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377588_comment'></div>医且欲大其疽而沽其直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377588_comment'></div>因以药稔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377588_comment'></div>而疽溃商毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377588_comment'></div>商之家诉于韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377588_comment'></div>韩侯尸其族而籍其有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377588_comment'></div>且二贼齧寿春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377588_comment'></div>陷颍上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377588_comment'></div>刷亳社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377588_comment'></div>掠合肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377588_comment'></div>经营于梁宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377588_comment'></div>其为老者杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377588_comment'></div>少者伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377588_comment'></div>驱人之妇女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377588_comment'></div>辇人之财货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1377588_comment'></div>将军固知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1377588_comment'></div>自将军受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1377588_comment'></div>迄今三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1377588_comment'></div>关东之惨毒不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1377588_comment'></div>杀伤驱辇之不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1377588_comment'></div>乃将军为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1377588_comment'></div>非君长仙芝之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1377588_comment'></div>文皇帝时卫公靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1377588_comment'></div>大帝时郑仁泰薛仁贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1377588_comment'></div>或戢敛不谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1377588_comment'></div>或伺候辎重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1377588_comment'></div>当时宪司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1377588_comment'></div>悉绳以法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1377588_comment'></div>今将军勋业不若卫公靖之多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1377588_comment'></div>出师非郑薛之敌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1377588_comment'></div>而横拥仕伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1377588_comment'></div>鞭挞馈运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1377588_comment'></div>以愚度之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1377588_comment'></div>将军之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1377588_comment'></div>酷于君长仙芝之行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1377588_comment'></div>甚为将军忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1377588_comment'></div>前者天子虑将军以爱子为念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1377588_comment'></div>复授禁秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1377588_comment'></div>俾在军前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1377588_comment'></div>则朝廷宠待将军倚望将军也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1377588_comment'></div>俱不浅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1377588_comment'></div>苟将军戮力以除暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1377588_comment'></div>推诚以报国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1377588_comment'></div>今其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1377588_comment'></div>无使蹑韩之医。</div><div id='poem_sentence_92_1377588_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
代县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='de246e9e18b94c62bc7f7b8a4c830b01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("de246e9e18b94c62bc7f7b8a4c830b01");'><span id='de246e9e18b94c62bc7f7b8a4c830b01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年</a>，44岁</div><div id='de246e9e18b94c62bc7f7b8a4c830b01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年</a>　曾一度北游晋地，过雁门关，有诗。作品：边夜。<div id='poem_38171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>边夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（876年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38171")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38171'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38171'>光景漂如水，生涯转似萍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38171'>雁门穷朔路，牛斗故乡星。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38171'>句尽人<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作书罢愁）</span>谁切，歌终泪自零。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38171'>夜阑回首算，何处不长亭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38171_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38171'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38171_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
蓟县
-----detail

-----title
蕲春
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d3b4aeb6930b4977b7cf132f320c39d4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d3b4aeb6930b4977b7cf132f320c39d4");'><span id='d3b4aeb6930b4977b7cf132f320c39d4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>，46岁</div><div id='d3b4aeb6930b4977b7cf132f320c39d4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=878&endYear=878')">878年</a>　在蕲州行卷刺史裴渥。作品：投蕲州裴员外启。<div id='poem_1377599' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377599' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377599?labeling=true' target='_blank'>投蕲州裴员外启</a><span class='authorDate'>（878年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377599")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377599_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377599'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377599'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377599_comment'></div>某月六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377599_comment'></div>辄以所著谗书一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377599_comment'></div>贡于客次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377599_comment'></div>遂归逆旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377599_comment'></div>载轸危途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377599_comment'></div>必恐员外以其姓氏单寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377599_comment'></div>精神钝滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377599_comment'></div>汨在众人之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377599_comment'></div>遗于繁务之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377599_comment'></div>某怀璧经穿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377599_comment'></div>壮年见志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377599_comment'></div>仲舒养勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377599_comment'></div>何啻三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377599_comment'></div>安世补亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377599_comment'></div>宁惟一箧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377599_comment'></div>其后因从计吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377599_comment'></div>遂混时人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377599_comment'></div>愤龙尾以不焦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377599_comment'></div>念鱼腮之屡曝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377599_comment'></div>嵇康骨俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377599_comment'></div>徒矜养性之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377599_comment'></div>李广数奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377599_comment'></div>岂是用兵之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377599_comment'></div>事往难问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377599_comment'></div>天高不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377599_comment'></div>去年牵迫旨甘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377599_comment'></div>留连江徼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377599_comment'></div>虽伤弓之鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377599_comment'></div>诚则恶弦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377599_comment'></div>食堇之虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377599_comment'></div>未能忘苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377599_comment'></div>所以远辞蜗舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377599_comment'></div>来谒龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377599_comment'></div>黍谷棠阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377599_comment'></div>方偕志愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377599_comment'></div>荷衣蕙带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377599_comment'></div>不奈风霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377599_comment'></div>负所业以长嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377599_comment'></div>向良工而有喟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377599_comment'></div>昔也松苗各性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377599_comment'></div>已知难进之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377599_comment'></div>今则火木相生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377599_comment'></div>未测自焚之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377599_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1377599_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=887&endYear=887')">887年9月</a>　九月，高骈被杀，隐著诗文讽刺。作品：妖乱志。题延和阁。<div id='poem_5324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_5324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/5324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>延和阁诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（881年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_5324_0'>① 高骈末年，惑于神仙之术。起延和阁于大厅之西，七间，高八丈，饰以珠玉，绮窗绣户，殆非人工。每旦，焚名香，祈王母之降。及毕师铎乱，人有登之者，于藻井垂莲之上，见二十八字云。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=893&endYear=893')">893年8月</a>　八月聂师道为歙州解围，隐有诗寄师道。作品：寄聂师道。<div id='poem_37788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_37788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37788'>欲芟荆棘种交梨，指画城中日恐迟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=893&endYear=893')">893年11月</a>　十一月，罗城成，隐作记。作品：杭州罗城记。<div id='poem_1377614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东安镇新筑罗城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（893年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377614")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377614'>天下自懿考僖皇之后。纲领不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377614_comment'></div>庞勋王郢抵触于前。仙芝君长践踏于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377614_comment'></div>寻乃黄巢大掠于京城。所以齐寇攘臂一噪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377614_comment'></div>四海瓦解。自尔枝牵蔓引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377614_comment'></div>耳闻口吠。其或一垒之不谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377614_comment'></div>一版之不严。则刳剔之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377614_comment'></div>虽十室之邑。三户之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377614_comment'></div>必壁堑以备之。篱落以抗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377614_comment'></div>况大藩之襟带。吾土之翳倚者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377614_comment'></div>杭之别部。旧有八都之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377614_comment'></div>其始以破山偷旌八将之功所致也。而东安主领太师杜公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377614_comment'></div>寻以擒逆贼薛朗于京口。破丁从实于毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377614_comment'></div>天子宠之。拜常州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377614_comment'></div>遂属其兵于子弟焉。抚于内者曰建思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377614_comment'></div>御于外而弭寇摧凶者曰建徽。经度于季孟之间者曰建威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377614_comment'></div>洎太师解印而归。淮叛淝偷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377614_comment'></div>连压封部。元帅大丞相彭城王始授君以板筑之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377614_comment'></div>濠堑之广袤。地里之横亘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377614_comment'></div>皆取则于丞相。一之日鸠其人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377614_comment'></div>相其险易。惟帅有令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377614_comment'></div>众克从之。二之日度其资费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377614_comment'></div>卜其力用。经之营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377614_comment'></div>厥画惟禀。三之日命其将李可球胡瑾等曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377614_comment'></div>汝常从役于杭。必能识大丞相意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377614_comment'></div>善匠事。勿令不如丞相指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377614_comment'></div>曰侔汝工。曰温汝率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377614_comment'></div>铎令等二十一将翼侔以进曰。曰𨛶洎俨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377614_comment'></div>汝督防遏备御二都之士卒。以介于侔之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377614_comment'></div>曰勋汝司吾储廪。谨吾出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377614_comment'></div>城者若有坠。惟汝之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377614_comment'></div>起大顺辛亥年秋七月壬戌。讫于明年夏四月庚寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377614_comment'></div>蟠东矗西。离连坎接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377614_comment'></div>隆者就之。洼者盈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377614_comment'></div>民不弛担。时不妨农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377614_comment'></div>夏五月。太师犒群帅于城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377614_comment'></div>若杵若畚者皆与焉。不三四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377614_comment'></div>淮南节度杨氏行密以称盗豕突猘冲。扰我疆境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377614_comment'></div>而东安尤为其所忌。行密减安仁义之精锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377614_comment'></div>分田頵陶雅金威之敢勇。以攻东安城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377614_comment'></div>楼橹翔空。矢石交迸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377614_comment'></div>翊日。我军凭其城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377614_comment'></div>毙贼将于城下者其数盈千。濠塞堑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377614_comment'></div>自是群寇不复有图南之意。是知人非城则无以为捍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377614_comment'></div>城非人则无以自固。不有城也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377614_comment'></div>人何以安。不有将也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377614_comment'></div>城何以坚。于时紫溪窜堡火口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377614_comment'></div>建宁下守。静江无将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377614_comment'></div>奔我而活者。四镇之生聚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377614_comment'></div>噫。天下之无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377614_comment'></div>吾乡则有河间凌准宗一濮阳吴降下已汝南袁不纳还朴以文学进。天下之有事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377614_comment'></div>吾乡则有太师建徽伯仲及诸将佐以武艺称。岂文武之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377614_comment'></div>倚伏而然也。抑江山禀受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377614_comment'></div>与时消息者乎。隐亦常以先师之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377614_comment'></div>干名贡府。进取未半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377614_comment'></div>九鼎羹沸。文既不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377614_comment'></div>武非所习。今则老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377614_comment'></div>高谢三军。太师以镌金勒石见徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377614_comment'></div>不敢坚逊。乾宁五年六月二十一日记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377614_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1377614_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=893&endYear=893')">893年</a>　有诗寄京城陆扆兄弟。作品：寄京阙陆郎中昆仲。<div id='poem_38058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=895&endYear=895')">895年</a>　冬终郊，钱镠奏封胥山伍子胥为惠应侯，隐为作碑文。作品：封胥山祠碑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=896&endYear=896')">896年7月</a>　七月，唐昭宗播迁，隐作诗自嘲；与钱镠唱和，常借机讽其出身，钱亦不怒。作品：感弄猴人赐朱绂。<div id='poem_37802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感弄猴人赐朱绂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（896年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37802")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_37802_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_37802_0'>① 《幕府燕闲录》云：“唐昭宗播迁，随驾伎艺人止有弄猴者，猴颇驯，能随班起居，昭宗赐以绯袍，号孙供奉，故罗隐有诗云云。朱梁篡位，取此猴，令殿下起居，猴望殿陛，见全忠，径趣其所，跳跃奋击，遂令杀之。”</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37802'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37802'>十二三年就试期，五湖烟月奈相违。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37802'>何如买取胡孙弄<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作学取孙供奉）</span>，一笑君王便著绯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37802'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_37802_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_37802'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(37802)'>评注</a><span id='poem_sentence_13_38196'>千门万户扃锁密，良匠不肯雕散材。<div id='poem_sentence_13_38196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_38196'>君今得意尚如此，况我麋鹿悠悠哉。<div id='poem_sentence_14_38196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_38196'>荣衰贵贱目所睹，莫嫌头白<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2660, "poem_sentence_15_38196")'>黄金台</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_38196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_38196'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_38196_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年</a>　送僧辩光，有诗。作品：送辩光大师。<div id='poem_38006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/38006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送𧦬光大<span class='inlineComment2'>（师以草书应制）</span>师</a><span class='authorDate'>（897年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_38006")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38006'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38006'>宁亲久别街西寺，待诏初离海<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作江）</span>上峰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38006'>一种苦心师得了，不须回首笑龙钟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38006'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38006_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年</a>　本年有诗称颂钱镠所建小楼。作品：尚父偶建小楼特摛丽藻绝句不敢称扬三首。<div id='poem_37761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚父偶建小楼特摛丽藻绝句不敢称扬三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（897年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_37761")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_37761_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_37761'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2660, "poem_allusion_37761")'>隗台</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_37761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37761'><div class='poemSentence' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/37762?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（897年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_37762_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_37762'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37762'>玳簪珠履愧非才，时凭阑干首重回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37762'>只待淮妖剪除后，别倾卮酒贺行台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37762_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_37763_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_37763'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1761, id='poem_sentence_1_37763'>风流孔令陶钧外，犹记山妖逼小台。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37763_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37763'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_37763_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年10月</a>　八月，唐昭宗赐钱镠铁券，十月，隐代钱镠作谢恩表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=898&endYear=898')">898年1月</a>　正月，隐应邀为吴公约作神道碑。作品：吴公约神道碑。<div id='poem_828761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_828761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/828761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴公约神道碑附诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（898年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_828761")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_828761_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_828761'>黄巢之将叛也。天下骚动。杭之豪杰。举挺以卫乡里者八人。故立八都之号。其间王公节将。派有分者一十三都。君居其一焉。君讳公约。字处仁。杭之馀杭人。以胆略为郡邑推。应募西讨。投西佳镇遏使。其后从董太尉御巢。加御史中丞。奏置都额。改硖石为郡邑之所。于是推锋破锐。勋业愈盛。由冬卿改秋曹民部二尚书。为将三十年。家无长物。出则督励士卒。入则训(阙二字)弟。斯亦名将之高节也。乾宁四年夏六月二十有一日。启手足于硖石之第。享年五十八。以明年正月十五日。卜宅于钱塘之新亭乡桐扣山之原。礼也。君嗣子以隐乡里之旧。请铭其墓。而复以诗一章。文其美于道之隅曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_828761_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_828761'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_828761'>吴山苍苍，吴水泱泱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_828761'>降生英灵，为公为王。<div id='poem_sentence_1_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_828761'>以严师旅，以奠封疆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_828761'>派有别者，我亦鹰扬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_828761'>取直之功，捍巢之绩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_828761'>虽从本军，实展良画。<div id='poem_sentence_5_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_828761'>践历禁旅，光扬事迹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_828761'>乃自西佳，迁于硖石。<div id='poem_sentence_7_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_828761'>上君东代，诸将西征。<div id='poem_sentence_8_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_828761'>贾其馀勇，资其锐兵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_828761'>稽山雾廓，京口波清。<div id='poem_sentence_10_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_828761'>再从貂冕，始拜冬卿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_828761'>吴会纷纭，淮右<span class='inlineComment2'>（从雍文华校本改）</span>奔竞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_828761'>驱其涷馁，犯我疆境。<div id='poem_sentence_13_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_828761'>躬励精卒，恭承上命。<div id='poem_sentence_14_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_828761'>雪霁松贞，风中草劲。<div id='poem_sentence_15_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_828761'>元戎承制，圣主酬劳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_828761'>大起名重，司元望高。<div id='poem_sentence_17_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_828761'>优游渥泽，出入官曹。<div id='poem_sentence_18_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_828761'>所谓鸡省，全资豹韬。<div id='poem_sentence_19_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_828761'>恭仰府城，载崇吾圉。<div id='poem_sentence_20_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_828761'>惟力是助，厥功以举。<div id='poem_sentence_21_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_828761'>云矗千堵，土攒万杵。<div id='poem_sentence_22_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_828761'>率以资产，役以军旅。<div id='poem_sentence_23_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_828761'>乃颁异宠，乃正华资。<div id='poem_sentence_24_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_828761'>大国纲纪，雄藩羽仪。<div id='poem_sentence_25_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_828761'>床间牛斗，杯里蛇疑。<div id='poem_sentence_26_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_828761'>天胡可测，神亦难知。<div id='poem_sentence_27_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_828761'>有仁于时，有功于物。<div id='poem_sentence_28_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_828761'>一代殊勋，二品清秩。<div id='poem_sentence_29_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_828761'>不谓不达，何获何失。<div id='poem_sentence_30_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_828761'>瑞马神羊，金箱玉室<span class='inlineComment2'>（出《全唐文》卷八九七。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_31_828761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_828761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_828761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=898&endYear=898')">898年6月</a>　六月，隐应邀作《东安镇新筑罗城记》<div id='poem_1377614' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377614' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377614?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东安镇新筑罗城记</a><span class='authorDate'>（893年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377614")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377614_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377614'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377614'>天下自懿考僖皇之后。纲领不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377614_comment'></div>庞勋王郢抵触于前。仙芝君长践踏于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377614_comment'></div>寻乃黄巢大掠于京城。所以齐寇攘臂一噪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377614_comment'></div>四海瓦解。自尔枝牵蔓引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377614_comment'></div>耳闻口吠。其或一垒之不谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377614_comment'></div>一版之不严。则刳剔之不暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377614_comment'></div>虽十室之邑。三户之乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377614_comment'></div>必壁堑以备之。篱落以抗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377614_comment'></div>况大藩之襟带。吾土之翳倚者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377614_comment'></div>杭之别部。旧有八都之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377614_comment'></div>其始以破山偷旌八将之功所致也。而东安主领太师杜公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377614_comment'></div>寻以擒逆贼薛朗于京口。破丁从实于毗陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377614_comment'></div>天子宠之。拜常州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377614_comment'></div>遂属其兵于子弟焉。抚于内者曰建思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377614_comment'></div>御于外而弭寇摧凶者曰建徽。经度于季孟之间者曰建威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377614_comment'></div>洎太师解印而归。淮叛淝偷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377614_comment'></div>连压封部。元帅大丞相彭城王始授君以板筑之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377614_comment'></div>濠堑之广袤。地里之横亘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377614_comment'></div>皆取则于丞相。一之日鸠其人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377614_comment'></div>相其险易。惟帅有令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377614_comment'></div>众克从之。二之日度其资费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377614_comment'></div>卜其力用。经之营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377614_comment'></div>厥画惟禀。三之日命其将李可球胡瑾等曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377614_comment'></div>汝常从役于杭。必能识大丞相意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377614_comment'></div>善匠事。勿令不如丞相指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377614_comment'></div>曰侔汝工。曰温汝率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377614_comment'></div>铎令等二十一将翼侔以进曰。曰𨛶洎俨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377614_comment'></div>汝督防遏备御二都之士卒。以介于侔之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377614_comment'></div>曰勋汝司吾储廪。谨吾出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377614_comment'></div>城者若有坠。惟汝之咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377614_comment'></div>起大顺辛亥年秋七月壬戌。讫于明年夏四月庚寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377614_comment'></div>蟠东矗西。离连坎接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377614_comment'></div>隆者就之。洼者盈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377614_comment'></div>民不弛担。时不妨农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377614_comment'></div>夏五月。太师犒群帅于城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377614_comment'></div>若杵若畚者皆与焉。不三四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377614_comment'></div>淮南节度杨氏行密以称盗豕突猘冲。扰我疆境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377614_comment'></div>而东安尤为其所忌。行密减安仁义之精锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377614_comment'></div>分田頵陶雅金威之敢勇。以攻东安城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377614_comment'></div>楼橹翔空。矢石交迸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377614_comment'></div>翊日。我军凭其城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377614_comment'></div>毙贼将于城下者其数盈千。濠塞堑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377614_comment'></div>自是群寇不复有图南之意。是知人非城则无以为捍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377614_comment'></div>城非人则无以自固。不有城也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377614_comment'></div>人何以安。不有将也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377614_comment'></div>城何以坚。于时紫溪窜堡火口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377614_comment'></div>建宁下守。静江无将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377614_comment'></div>奔我而活者。四镇之生聚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377614_comment'></div>噫。天下之无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377614_comment'></div>吾乡则有河间凌准宗一濮阳吴降下已汝南袁不纳还朴以文学进。天下之有事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377614_comment'></div>吾乡则有太师建徽伯仲及诸将佐以武艺称。岂文武之柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377614_comment'></div>倚伏而然也。抑江山禀受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377614_comment'></div>与时消息者乎。隐亦常以先师之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377614_comment'></div>干名贡府。进取未半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377614_comment'></div>九鼎羹沸。文既不用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377614_comment'></div>武非所习。今则老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377614_comment'></div>高谢三军。太师以镌金勒石见徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377614_comment'></div>不敢坚逊。乾宁五年六月二十一日记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_38130_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年10月</a>　钱镠建镇海军使院，冬十月，命隐作记。作品：镇海军使院记。<div id='poem_1377613' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377613' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377613?labeling=true' target='_blank'>镇海军使院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（900年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377613")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377613_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377613'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377613'>惟天子建国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377613_comment'></div>必维九牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377613_comment'></div>九牧既序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377613_comment'></div>区分局署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377613_comment'></div>两汉三公府有掾属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377613_comment'></div>魏晋而降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377613_comment'></div>则置行台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377613_comment'></div>若魏以秦王仪镇中都<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作山）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377613_comment'></div>高齐以辛术监治东徐州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377613_comment'></div>皆行台之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377613_comment'></div>其官属则令仆以至于尚书丞郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377613_comment'></div>唐制由行台而置采访使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377613_comment'></div>殆今节制之始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377613_comment'></div>镇海军旧治京口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377613_comment'></div>大丞相以钱塘之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377613_comment'></div>东戡汉宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377613_comment'></div>西歼逆朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377613_comment'></div>天子不欲易其土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377613_comment'></div>故自符竹四命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377613_comment'></div>然后移军于钱塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377613_comment'></div>生物以宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377613_comment'></div>租赋以便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377613_comment'></div>斥去旧址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377613_comment'></div>广以新规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1377613_comment'></div>廓开闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1377613_comment'></div>拔起阶级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1377613_comment'></div>俾幢节之气色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1377613_comment'></div>貔武之出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1377613_comment'></div>得以周旋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1377613_comment'></div>庚申年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1377613_comment'></div>加辟大厅之西南隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1377613_comment'></div>以为宾从晏息之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1377613_comment'></div>左界飞楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1377613_comment'></div>右劘严城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1377613_comment'></div>地耸势峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1377613_comment'></div>面约背敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1377613_comment'></div>肥楹巨栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1377613_comment'></div>间架相称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1377613_comment'></div>雕奂之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1377613_comment'></div>朱紫苒苒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1377613_comment'></div>非若越之今而润之旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1377613_comment'></div>疆埸之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1377613_comment'></div>则议之于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1377613_comment'></div>聘好之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1377613_comment'></div>则接之于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1377613_comment'></div>生民之疾痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1377613_comment'></div>则启之于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1377613_comment'></div>军旅之赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1377613_comment'></div>则参之于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1377613_comment'></div>非徒以酒食骈罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1377613_comment'></div>而语言嘲谑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1377613_comment'></div>其府属以下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1377613_comment'></div>或八都旧将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1377613_comment'></div>或从公于征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1377613_comment'></div>或禀之于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1377613_comment'></div>或拔之于乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1377613_comment'></div>故天子用清宫传道之选以佐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1377613_comment'></div>辍教民论道之任以副之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1377613_comment'></div>其馀省秩卿曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1377613_comment'></div>职领相次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1377613_comment'></div>自我朝藩服官属之盛无加也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1377613_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1377613_comment'></div>大丞相之勋德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1377613_comment'></div>既藏之天府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1377613_comment'></div>而攀鳞附翼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1377613_comment'></div>非镌刻乐石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1377613_comment'></div>其可久乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1377613_comment'></div>是年冬十月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1377613_comment'></div>始命观察判官罗隐为记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1377613_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript:
