ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年12月</a>　十二月，隐有诗表达作为御史中丞而无所作为的无奈心情。作品：冬暮城西晚眺。<div id='poem_37849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年9月</a>　秋九月，隐之诗友吴仁璧被钱镠沉江溺杀。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年</a>　春，赴大涤山悼道教大师闾丘方远，有诗。作品：题玄同先生草堂三首。<div id='poem_38147' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_38148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38148'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38148'>先生<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_1_38148'>意密寻难会，情深恨有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38148'>石桥春暖后，句漏药成初。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38148'>珍重云兼鹤，从来不定居。<div id='poem_sentence_3_38148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_38148'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38148_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_38149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_38149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_38149'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_38149'>常时忆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_38149", 38149, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>讨论</span>，历历事犹存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_38149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_38149'>酒向馀杭尽，云从大涤昏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_38149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_38149'>往来无道侣，归去有台恩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_38149'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_38149_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年8月</a>　八月，隐应黄滔之请为陈黯文集作后序。作品：陈先生集后序。<div id='poem_1377611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1377611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1377611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈先生集后序</a><span class='authorDate'>（902年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐末 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(19207, "唐末", "罗隐", "poem_title_1377611")'>罗隐</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1377611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1377611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1377611'>颍川陈先生讳黯字希孺。曩者与予声迹相接于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1377611_comment'></div>各获誉于进取。咸通庚寅岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1377611_comment'></div>胶其道于蒲津秋试之场。自后俱为小宗伯所困不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1377611_comment'></div>至甲申春。告予以婚嫁之牵制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1377611_comment'></div>东归青门操执之。后余亦东游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1377611_comment'></div>逮大梁时。故杭州卢员外浔在幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1377611_comment'></div>赍其文轴谓余曰。陈君罢而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1377611_comment'></div>岂其斯文之终窒乎。予东及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1377611_comment'></div>为我归其文而激其来。余至维扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1377611_comment'></div>及归其文。遵其言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1377611_comment'></div>相欢月而后别。为我谢范阳公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1377611_comment'></div>龙门之役。不复顾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1377611_comment'></div>由是音尘杜绝。天复元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1377611_comment'></div>四门博士江夏君通家相好。于吴越面余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1377611_comment'></div>论及场中曩之名士及希孺之表也。余不觉怆然怀旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1377611_comment'></div>明年。黄君以其文章德业为之序以寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1377611_comment'></div>俾予系述。遂得申斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1377611_comment'></div>呜呼。大唐设进士科三百年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1377611_comment'></div>得之者或非常之人。失之者或非常之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1377611_comment'></div>若陈希孺之才美。则非常之人失之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1377611_comment'></div>德行莫若敦于亲戚。文章莫若大于流传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1377611_comment'></div>今已备于江夏之笔矣。余不克再叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1377611_comment'></div>止书交道于是。噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1377611_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1377611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年9月</a>　九月，隐与皮日休以酒令共解杭州之围。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年</a>　与九华故人相聚两旬。作品：送人归湘中兼寄旧知。<div id='poem_37974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_38022_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_38022'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=909&endYear=909')">909年</a>　临终前有诗感别钱镠。作品：感别元帅尚父。<div id='poem_38127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_38127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_38127'>疲牛<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(7846, "poem_sentence_2_38127")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_38127", 38127, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>舐犊</span></span>心犹切，阴鹤鸣雏力已衰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_38127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_38127'>稚子不才身抱疾，日窥贞<span id='poem_sentence_4_38127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=909&endYear=909')">909年12月13日</a>　迁盐铁发运使；十二月十三日巳时，殁于西阙舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=910&endYear=910')">910年1月</a>　春，归灵于杭州钱塘县定山乡居山里，殡于徐村之穴，镇海军节度推官金部郎中沈崧为撰墓志，僧归仁有悼诗。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
南京（金陵）

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=885&endYear=885')">885年</a>　本年前后，隐有《乱后逢友人》诗；本年或稍后，朝贤议欲召隐为朝官，为大臣韦贻范所阻。<div id='poem_37888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_37888'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_37888'>沧海去未得，倚舟聊问津。<div id='poem_sentence_0_37888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_37888'>生灵寇盗尽，方镇改更贫<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作频）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_37888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_37888'>梦里旧行处，眼前新贵人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_37888_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_37888'>从来事如此，君莫独沾巾。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=886&endYear=886')">886年</a>　病寄南徐，有诗送刘校书兼寄歙州刺史吴园。作品：送刘校书之新安寄吴常侍。<div id='poem_37982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_37982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
